 The demonetization process has been implemented to curb the black economy and eliminate black money in the country
 arthvyavastha main kul karency kaa lagbhag 86 fisadi karency 500 or 1000 rupee kii note main thi jise gaiyrkanoonee ghoshit kiya ja chukaa he
 Now the government is trying to move the economy towards cashless transaction where digital transaction is to be preferred
 jaaniye cash iconomi or cashles iconomi main kya he antar:cash tranjaction1
 Cash transaction is the oldest method of any purchase or sale
 desh kii arthvyavastha main 18 lakh karod rupee kii karencydimonetigeshan prakriyashuru hone ke pehle thi
 At the same time, the government is estimated to be present in the black economy, about more than 84 lakh crore rupees
 2
 The largest denomination (currency of 500, 1000, 2000 rupees) proves to be helpful for making transactions easily using cash
 cash ke jariye tranjaction karne kaa sabase bada phayda ye he ki ukt tranjaction ko bank athwa sarkaar sechhipaakar kiya ja saktaa haior kanoon ke mutabik kisi tranjaction par dey tex se bhi bachaa ja saktaa he
 3
 cash tranjaction behad aasaan tarika he
 Here, only currency is needed in exchange for any purchase
 cash tranjaction ko aasaan isliye mana jaataa he ki yahaan mahaj karency ke aadan-pradaan par tranjaction puraa maan liya jaataa he
 In this medium, only the buyer needs to have the currency and the seller only has the product
 cashles tranjaction1
 Cashless transactions are an increasingly popular medium of digitization
 is madhyam se kharidari athwa bikwaali karne ke liye donon kharidaar or bechney vaale ko bank kaa sahaara lene kii jarurat padati he
 Along with your bank, the Reserve Bank and the government's tax department also play an important role in this medium
 2
 Plastic money or credit and debit are used for cashless transactions
 yah card kisi bank main acount kholane par diya jaataa he
 In addition, bank checks and drafts fall under the category of cashless transactions
 digital wolet, mobile banking, enift or artijies bhi cashles tranjaction ke teji se popyular hote tareeke hai
 3
 cashles tranjaction main cash jaisi aasaani nahin dekhne ko milti he
 But in terms of security, it is much better than giving cash
 is madhyam main bank or sarkaar ke kar vibhaag kii najar main prayek bade tranjaction rahete hai
 At the same time, full details of even the smallest transactions are available
 cashles banaam cash1
 During the last five years, there has been a 1000-fold increase in mobile banking in the country
 2
 Cashless transfers through NEFT have increased 20 times over the past five years
 3
 RTGS and check payments in banking have doubled during the last five years
 4
 Check payments and net banking have declined over the past five years
 5
 Until five years ago, three-fourths of payments were made through banking checks in the banking system
 ab cash tranjaction or cashles tranjaction kii in suvidhaon or dikkaton ko dhyaan main rakhte hue sarkaar or rigerv bank kii koshish he ki desh ko cash se cashles iconomi kii taraf badhaayaa aage jaae
 However, for this it is very important that banking should be more popular in the country

 chaay banane ke baad hamamen se zyaadaatar logon ke gharon main ujd chipatti ko koodaydaan main phenk diya jaataa he
 But do you know that this tea leaf can be reused in many ways
 yun to ujd chipatti ko kai tarah se dobaaraa istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
 But it is very important that you know the right way to use it
 chaay banane ke baad channi main bachi hui chipatti ko acchhee tarah se saaf kar len
 So that the sweetness present in it goes away
 bachi hui chipatti ko in kaamon main istemaal kar sakate hai:1
 Anti-oxidants are found in tea leaves
 aise main chot yaa kisi jakhm par chipatti kaa lep lagaana phydemand rahata he
 Wash the boiled tea leaves thoroughly
 ise chot par lagane se ghaav jaldi bhar jayega
 Also, if you wish, wash the tea leaves and boil them again
 is pani se ghaav dhonaa bhi phydemand rahegaa
 2
 chipatti kaa pani ek behtareen condishnar hota he
 Wash the tea leaves and boil them again
 is pani se baalo ko dhoen
 This will make it shiny and soft
 3
 Wash and dry the tea leaves again
 kabuli chane banaate samay is chipatti kaa istemaal kiya ja saktaa he
 This will improve the color of the gram
 4
 Boil this tea leaf again
 is pani ko ek spray bottle main bharkar, furniture kii safai karen
 This will brighten the furniture
 5
 Clean the remaining tea leaves thoroughly
 is chipatti kaa istemaal khaad ke rup main bhi kiya ja saktaa he

 Prime Minister Manmohan Singh left for a five-day visit to Japan and Thailand on Monday
 yah yatra ‘purv kii ore dekho’ niti ko nayaa arth dene tathaa asia prashanth main shanti, samruddhi or sthirataa main yogadan dene kii ummid se par kendrit he
 Manmohan flew to Tokyo for his first stop
 unhone japan ko ‘bharat ke liye mahatvapurn kshetreey evam vaishvik saajhedaar’ bataaya
 Before leaving, Manmohan said in his statement that he would talk about strengthening India's relations with Japan in the political, security and energy sectors
 unhone kaha, ‘meri japan or thailand yatra se hamaari ‘purv kii ore dekho niti’ majboot hogi tathaa ise nayaa arth milegaa
 During the three-day visit to Japan, Manmohan will discuss furthering the bilateral agreement for deepening defense ties and for cooperation on civil nuclear agreement
 pradhanmantri buudhvaar ko vibhinn muddon par mejabaan pradhanmantri shinjo abe ke saath vistaar se vichaar-vimarsh karenge
 During this time special attention will be given to increasing cooperation in defense, economic, energy and other fields
 pradhanmantri ne kaha, ‘hamaare hiton kaa saamanjasy bad rahaa he or main is sambandh ko asia main sthai shanti evam samruddhi ke liye apane nazariye ke jaruri tatv ke rup main dekhtaa hum
 Singh described Japanese Prime Minister Abe as a very good friend and said that he would further strengthen the momentum that india-japan strategic and global partnership has gained from frequent summits between the two countries
 asainya parmaanu sahyog qaraar ke bare main singh ne japani samvaadadaataaon se kaha ki japan main samasyaayein hai or vahaan is saal ke aakhir main ucch sadan ke liye chunaav hone hai
 He said, "but i hope we can make progress in civil nuclear energy cooperation
" ’ singh ne kaha ‘meri koshish hogi ki is yatra kaa upyog main hamaari ranneetik or vaishvik bhagidaari ko majboot karne ke liye karun, jisamen asainya parmaanu urja sahyog ke sandarbh main ek samjhaute tak pahunchane kii koshish shaamil he
 Since the Fukushima nuclear accident in Japan in March 2011, negotiations for a civil nuclear cooperation agreement have not progressed as expected
 bharat america parmaanu qaraar kaa or antarrashtriya praudyogiki pratibandhon se bharat ko chhot die jane kaa japan ne swaagat kiya he
 On the other hand, the governments there have found it difficult to garner political support due to the intense opposition to the non-proliferation camp
 japan dwaara parmaanu upkaran or praudyogiki kii bharat ko bikri par bharat ke purv parmaanu pareekshanon, parmaanu aprasar sandhi tathaa vyapak pareekshan pratibandh sandhi (CTBT) par hastakshar se nai dilli ke lagaataar inkaar ke chalate is aadhaar par asar padaa he ki yah sab bhedbhaavpurn he

 sadiyon pehle janm lene vaali libral arts ko shuru main aise subjects kaa mishran mana jaataa tha jo kisi bhi insaan ko 'nolejeble' banane kaa kaam karte hai
 Liberal education first began in the seventh century BC
 iskaa uddeshy corcej se judi sabhi tarah kii simaaon ko khatm karnaa tha
 According to the Association of American Colleges and Universities, the definition of Liberal Education is, 'such a philosophy of education that empowers a person with a strong understanding of knowledge and transferable skills and values, ethics and civic management
 isaki khaasiyat ahm muddon kaa chunauteepurn tareeke se saamana karnaa he or yah kisi khaas course yaa study se itar study kii alag raah he
 'liberal education allows students to connect with different fields and by this they can be equipped with a wider perspective
 bharat main jahaan ek subject main degree lenaa popular he, vahaan libral ajukeshan ab dhire-dhire apni jagah bana rahi he
 It is often argued that it is better to know a subject in depth than to know a little about different subjects
 lekin libral ajukeshan kaa matlab yah nahin he ki anya degree corcej ke mukaable study kam mehnat vaali yaa kam kendrit hoti he
 The only difference is that it identifies the value addition that can be achieved by combining different subjects together
 bharat main libral ajukeshnalibaral arts ko lekar bharat main akasar kanfusion rahata he
 In the literal sense, Liberal Education refers to 'freedom' from education, and Liberal Arts is seen as a study of social sciences and humanities
 lekin, libral ajukeshan kaa concept hamaari viraasat kaa ek hissaa rahaa he
 Centuries ago, Gurukuls were established across the country on the basis of this principle

 madhyapradesh kii alag alag mandiyon main rakhaa hajaaron quintal gehun is barish kii bhent chadh gaya
 This is the fastest rainfall in Mandsaur district during the month of April in the last 10 years
 mandsaur main mangalvaar dopaher achaanak hui barish main hajaaron quintal anaaj barish main bhig gaya
 Farmers allege that if the mandi committee wanted it, it could have already auctioned the food grains outside
 jisase barish se hue nuksaan ko taala ja saktaa tha
 But the Mandi Committee auctioned the grains lying in the first shed due to which thousands of quintal wheat and gram crops lying outside have suffered heavy losses
 is maamle main jab mandi sachiv o
 P
 sharma se baat kii to unhone saaf kah diya ki prakritik aapadaa main mandi kya kar sakati he, lekin phir baat ko sambhalate hue yah bhi kaha ki khule main pade gehun ko shed main rakhwane kii vyavastha kii ja rahi he
 On the other hand in Madhya Pradesh's Sheopur also, after a sudden change in the weather, rains with strong wind in the late evening wreaked havoc
